***nope.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nope.html>nope</a> (13156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1"><a href = vnd.unilang:etymology.html>Etymology</a> 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:represent.html>Representing</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:no.html>no</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:pronounce.html>pronounced</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mouth.html>mouth</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:snap.html>snapped</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:close.html>closed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:end.html>end</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:yep.html>yep</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">welp</i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:nope.html>nope</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:informal.html>informal</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:no.html>No</a>.
<ul><li><b>1856</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sidney.html>Sidney</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:george.html>George</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fisher.html>Fisher</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:charles.html>Charles</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:edward.html>Edward</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fisher.html>Fisher</a>, <i>Kanzas <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:constitution.html>Constitution</a></i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=FzYPAAAAIAAJamp;vid=OCLC05086871amp;dq=nopeamp;q=nope+date%3A1856-1856amp;pgis=1"><a href = vnd.unilang:p.html>p</a>. 97</a>,
<dl><dd>"<a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:my.html>my</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:son.html>son</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:here.html>here</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:clarence.html>Clarence</a>?" <a href = vnd.unilang:ask.html>asked</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roger.html>Roger</a> Oakley.
